<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тосковать.html>тоскова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">toskovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затосковать.html>затоскова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zatoskovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + dative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to start to miss, to start to yearn for</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to start to plaintively express longing for</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заточить.html>заточи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zatočítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sharpen</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заточка.html>зато́чка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zatóčka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заточка.html>зато́чки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заточка.html>зато́чки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заточка.html>зато́чек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sharpening <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a tool, a knife, a pencil</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>, grinding <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">an edge on a blade</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">criminal  slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a self-made stabbing weapon; shiv, shank</li></ol>

***затравить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:затравить.html>затрави́ть</a> (17442)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:травить.html>трави́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">travítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затравить.html>затрави́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zatravítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:травить.html>трави́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">затра́вливать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hunt down, to bring to bay</li>
<li>to badger, to intimidate, to make someone's life miserable, to leave no breathing space</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:затрагивать.html>затра́гивать</a> (13278)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">затро́г-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zatróg-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затрагивать.html>затра́гивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zatrágivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затронуть.html>затро́нуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to touch, to affect
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:затрагивать.html>затра́гивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:больной.html>больно́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zatrágivatʹ</b> bolʹnóje mésto</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to touch smb on the raw; touch a sore spot</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to affect, to wound
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:затрагивать.html>затра́гивать</a></b> чьё-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:самолюбие.html>самолю́бие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zatrágivatʹ</b> čʹjó-libo samoljúbije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to wound smb's self-esteem</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to touch <i>(upon)</i>, to deal <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:затрагивать.html>затра́гивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вопрос.html>вопро́с</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zatrágivatʹ</b> voprós (o)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to touch upon the issue (of)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to affect, to infringe
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:затрагивать.html>затра́гивать</a></b> чьи́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:интерес.html>интере́сы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zatrágivatʹ</b> čʹí-libo interésy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to infringe (on) smb's interests</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:требовать.html>тре́бовать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trébovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затребовать.html>затре́бовать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zatrébovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>

***затронуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:затронуть.html>затро́нуть</a> (11815)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тронуть.html>тро́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trónutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затронуть.html>затро́нуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zatrónutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затрагивать.html>затра́гивать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">затро́гивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to touch, to affect
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>неё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:затронутый.html>затро́нуты</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:легкое.html>лёгкие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nejó <b>zatrónuty</b> ljóxkije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">her lungs are affected</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:затронуть.html>затро́нуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:больной.html>больно́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zatrónutʹ</b> bolʹnóje mésto</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to touch smb on the raw; touch a sore spot</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to affect, to wound
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:затронуть.html>затро́нуть</a></b> чьё-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:самолюбие.html>самолю́бие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zatrónutʹ</b> čʹjó-libo samoljúbije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to wound smb's self-esteem</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to touch <i>(upon)</i>, to deal <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:затронуть.html>затро́нуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вопрос.html>вопро́с</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zatrónutʹ</b> voprós (o)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to touch upon the issue (of)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to affect, to infringe
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:затронуть.html>затро́нуть</a></b> чьи́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:интерес.html>интере́сы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zatrónutʹ</b> čʹí-libo interésy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to infringe (on) smb's interests</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***затруднить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:затруднить.html>затрудни́ть</a> (12180)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трудный.html>тру́дный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trúdnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затруднить.html>затрудни́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zatrudnítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затруднять.html>затрудня́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hamper, to impede, to complicate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:затруднить.html>затрудни́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:доступ.html>до́ступ</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> чему́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zatrudnítʹ</b> dóstup k čemú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to complicate access to smth</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to give/cause someone trouble, to make difficulties <i>(for)</i>, to embarrass
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вас</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:затруднить.html>затрудни́т</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éto vas ne <b>zatrudnít</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">would you mind doing it?</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:затруднять.html>затрудня́ть</a> (15019)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затруднить.html>затрудни́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zatrudnítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затруднять.html>затрудня́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zatrudnjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:затруднить.html>затрудни́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hamper, to impede, to complicate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:затруднять.html>затрудня́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:движение.html>движе́ния</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:одежда.html>оде́жде</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> т.п.)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zatrudnjátʹ</b> dvižénija (ob odéžde i t.p.)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hamper smb's movement</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to give/cause someone trouble, to make difficulties <i>(for)</i>, to embarrass</li></ol>
